### TilesPostData\<T\>

```ts
type TilesPostData<T> =
  {
    DeviceIDs: number | readonly number[]
  } & T extends DeviceType ?
    {
      SelectedBuilding: number
      SelectedDevice: number
    }
  : {
      SelectedBuilding: null
      SelectedDevice: null
    }
```
